--- Commit Message ---
LU-19481 lov: skip parity mirrors for normal read/write IOs

Add lre_parity flag to track mirrors containing parity
components. Skip these mirrors during normal read and
write operations, but allow designated mirror IOs to
access them.

Signed-off-by: Patrick Farrell <pfarrell@whamcloud.com>

## Summary

**Fix Applied:** Removed the unused variable `mirror_id` declaration on line 3577 in `lustre/utils/liblustreapi_layout.c`.

**Rationale:** 
The variable `uint32_t mirror_id;` was declared inside the `list_for_each_entry` loop in the `llapi_layout_merge()` function but was never actually used anywhere in the loop body. This triggered a compilation error because the build is configured with `-Werror=unused-variable`, which treats unused variable warnings as errors.

The variable appears to be leftover from previous code or was declared with the intention of being used but ultimately wasn't needed. The patch you applied doesn't reference this variable, so it's safe to remove. The function works correctly without it - mirror IDs are handled through `mirror_id_offset` and the component's `llc_mirror_id` field directly.
